**GT:** `7.773814951275034*epsilon**3 + 55.12431765498469*epsilon**0.26636900997297436*exp(-52.48673409660327/(8.314*T)) + epsilon*3.8053996848046987*sin(T - 276.43885211152184)`

The GT has three terms:
1. `c0*epsilon**3` — a cubic term in epsilon
2. `c2*epsilon**c3*exp(-c4/(c5*T))` — a fractional power of epsilon times a Boltzmann-like exponential in T
3. `epsilon*c6*sin(T - c7)` — epsilon times a sinusoidal function of T

Key basis functions: `epsilon**3`, `epsilon**~0.27 * exp(-const/T)`, `epsilon*sin(T - const)`

The sin(T - c7) term can be expanded as `epsilon*(A*sin(T) + B*cos(T))`.

Let me analyze each candidate:

**Candidate 1:** `T*c0 + c1*epsilon**(1/4) + c2 + c3*epsilon**3 + c4*epsilon**5*log(c5*epsilon + 1)*cos(T*c6) + c7*epsilon`
- Has T*c0 (linear in T alone) — can set c0=0
- Has epsilon**(1/4) instead of epsilon**~0.27 — fixed exponent, can't match
- cos(T*c6) instead of sin(T-c7) — could match sin with phase shift, but multiplied by epsilon**5*log(...) instead of epsilon
- Missing exp(-c4/(c5*T)) term
Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 2:** `c0 + c1*log(c2*epsilon + 1)*cos(T*c3) + c4*epsilon**3 + c5*epsilon*exp(T*c6/(T + c7)) + c8*epsilon**c9`
- Has epsilon**3 ✓
- Has epsilon**c9 — free exponent, could match ~0.27
- Has epsilon*exp(T*c6/(T+c7)): T*c6/(T+c7) = c6/(1+c7/T). For this to equal -c4/(c5*T), we'd need c6/(1+c7/T) ≈ -const/T. As T→∞, c6/(1+c7/T)→c6, which is constant, not going to 0. So exp(T*c6/(T+c7)) → exp(c6), a constant. This can't match exp(-const/T) exactly for all T.
  Actually, T*c6/(T+c7) = c6*T/(T+c7) = c6/(1+c7/T). If c6=0, the exp term becomes 1, giving c5*epsilon. Meanwhile exp(-const/T) is not a constant. So this can't reproduce the GT's T-dependence in the second term.
- log(c2*epsilon+1)*cos(T*c3): This has cos(T*c3) which could provide oscillatory T dependence, but log(c2*epsilon+1) ≠ epsilon for all epsilon.
- Missing sin(T)*epsilon term
Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 3:** `T*c0 + c1*exp(c2*epsilon) + c3 + c4*log(c5*epsilon + 1)*cos(T*c6) + c7*epsilon**3 + c8*log(T*c9 + 1)*Abs(epsilon)**(1/4)`
- T*c0: set c0=0
- exp(c2*epsilon): set c1=0 or c2=0 → constant
- log(c5*epsilon+1)*cos(T*c6): not epsilon*sin(T-c7)
- log(T*c9+1)*|epsilon|^(1/4): not epsilon^0.27*exp(-const/T)
- Missing the right T-dependence structures
Candidate 3 verdict: [NO MATCH]

- exp(c7*epsilon)*cos(T*c8) mixes epsilon and T wrong way
